# Body-Base-Example — Các Case Extreme Tiết Lộ Kiến Trúc Body-Base

> **Một người workaholic burnout → reveals which channels were starved.**
> **Một digital nomad rong ruổi 10 năm → reveals what nature over-feeds và
> what social depth it doesn't provide.**
> **Một tín đồ bán cả gia sản theo đạo → reveals meaning channel over-fed
> at cost of family bonding và body care.**
> **Một nghệ nhân lacquer 40 năm không nghỉ → reveals craft mastery chunk
> sustainability.**
> **Một tỷ phú thành công bỗng thấy "trống rỗng" → reveals what money
> channel doesn't feed.**
>
> Đây là **methodology qua extreme cases** — thay vì tìm channels qua
> trung bình dân số (quá nhiều noise), isolate signal qua những
> individuals nơi MỘT channel dominant và others neglected. Mỗi case
> = two data points về channel architecture: (1) what over-fed channel
> provides, (2) what starved channels would have provided (revealed
> through consequences).

---

> **Trạng thái:** OUTLINE v1.0 — Phase A complete, content fill Phase B
> **Ngày:** 2026-04-14
> **Mục đích:** Data file với 30-50 extreme passion/survival cases
> providing empirical grounding cho Body-Base.md channel architecture.
> Parallel to Feel-Example-Draft.md role trong Feeling/ folder.
> **Vị trí:** Core-Deep-Dive/Body-Base/ (data file, referenced heavily
> by Body-Base.md §4, §9)
> **Flow đọc:**
>   Body-Base.md (foundation file — what channels exist)
>   ├── Body-Base-Example.md (THIS FILE — cases validating channels)
>   └── [...other Body-Base/ files...]
> **Tiền đề:**
>   Body-Base.md §4 (channel enumeration)
>   Body-Base.md §9 (individual variation principle)
>   Calibration-Inputs-Analysis.md §4 (existing survival cases — WILL
>     BE ABSORBED INTO §11)
>   Feel-Example-Draft.md §9b (drive chunks — E117-E124 compound với
>     body-base channels)
> **Quy ước:** 🟢 Research/documented case | 🟡 General pattern |
>    🔴 Hypothesis case
> **⚠️ NO PERSONAL INFO rule:** Examples use general patterns or
>    documented public cases. Anonymous where possible.

- §7 — MASTERY/KNOWLEDGE EXTREMES (B26-B30)
- §8 — CONSUMPTION EXTREMES (B31-B35)
- §9 — STATUS/POWER EXTREMES (B36-B40)
- §10 — EXPRESSION/CREATION EXTREMES (B41-B44)
- §11 — SURVIVAL EXTREMES (B45-B50) — absorbed từ Calibration-Inputs
- §12 — CROSS-CASE PATTERN ANALYSIS
- §13 — CHANNEL ARCHITECTURE REVEALED
- §14 — GAPS DISCOVERED (framework refinement)
- §15 — SOURCES

---

## §0 — METHODOLOGY: WHY EXTREME CASES

[Phase B fill]

### §0.1 The problem with average-population studies

Traditional approach: survey N people, measure happiness/wellbeing,
correlate với variables. **Problems**:
- Most people multi-channel balanced (smoothing)
- Individual variation lost in averaging
- Silent channels (nature, movement, etc.) don't produce clear
  signal to measure
- Cultural noise obscures underlying biology
- Cannot isolate contribution of any single channel

Result: decades of research gives mixed findings on questions like
"do humans need nature?" — signal lost in noise.

### §0.2 Signal isolation via extreme cases

**Alternative approach**: find individuals where ONE channel
dramatically dominant, others dramatically starved. The imbalance
reveals:

**(1) What over-fed channel provides** (why it's so rewarding to
that individual)

**(2) What starved channels would have provided** (revealed through
consequences, symptoms, "what's missing")

**(3) Substitutability limits** (why over-feeding one doesn't
compensate for starving others)

Classical scientific methodology: medical research uses this —
disease cases reveal normal function by showing what breaks when
function fails. Ablation studies, extreme variants, outliers all
provide signal that averaging hides.

### §0.3 Two types of extreme cases

**Passion extremes** (this file new contribution):
- Individual voluntarily over-feeds one channel
- Other channels often starved as consequence
- Consequences: burnout, emptiness after success, isolation,
  relational damage, health damage
- Reveals: channel architecture through imbalance

**Survival extremes** (absorbed từ Calibration-Inputs-Analysis §4):
- Individual forced/chose isolation in single environment
- Which channels present sustained life? Which absent?
- Reveals: channel substitutability và minimum requirements

**Complementary**:
- Passion extremes: show what each channel provides in abundance
- Survival extremes: show what each channel provides at minimum
- Together: complete picture of channel contributions

### §0.4 Information extraction per case

Each case = 2 data points về channel architecture:

```
                    │ Over-fed       │ Starved
────────────────────┼────────────────┼──────────────────
Case: Workaholic    │ Achievement    │ Body, social,
burnout             │ Meaning        │ nature, rest
                    │                │
Reveals:            │ What success   │ Why burnout hurts
                    │ feeds          │ so much —
                    │                │ accumulated
                    │                │ deficits
```

Multiple cases across categories → full channel architecture.

### §0.5 Specific value of "success-then-emptiness" cases

Particularly valuable: individuals who achieved their dominant-
channel goal và reported "trống rỗng" or similar:

- Billionaire achieves money goal → reports unexpected emptiness
- Olympic gold medalist → post-victory depression
- Fame seeker achieves recognition → finds it insufficient
- Academic completes PhD → reports loss of purpose

These reveal **exactly what achievement doesn't provide**. Each
"trống rỗng" = direct evidence of starved channels that expected
achievement would feed but didn't. High-signal data.

### §0.6 Distinction từ Feel-Example-Draft §9b approach

Feel-Example-Draft §9b covered drive chunks (E117-E124) — what
drives people to extreme engagement. THIS file covers **channel
consequences** of extreme engagement:

- Feel-Example-Draft §9b: "This is what drives workaholism" (E118
  obsessive inquiry + E119 legacy + etc.)
- Body-Base-Example.md: "This is what workaholism's single-channel
  dominance REVEALS about other channels starving"

Complementary: drive explains why, body-base shows consequence on
channel architecture.

---

## §1 — PER-CASE SCHEMA

[Phase B fill guide]

Each case should follow this schema:

```markdown
### B[N]: [Short descriptive title]

**Scenario**: [Concrete description of case — can be general pattern
or documented public figure. NO PERSONAL INFO per rule.]

**Over-fed channel(s)**:
- Primary: [channel name] — [why dominant]
- Secondary: [channel] — [if applicable]

**Starved channel(s)**:
- [channel] — [evidence of starvation: symptoms, consequences]
- [channel] — [...]

**Consequences observed**:
- [symptom/outcome 1]
- [symptom/outcome 2]
- [...]

**Channel architecture revealed**:
[What this case tells us about body-base channels. What the over-fed
channel provides that other channels don't. What starved channels
would have provided. Substitutability limits.]

**Cross-reference**:
- Similar cases: [B-numbers]
- Contrasting cases: [B-numbers]
- Body-Base.md section: [which channel section this validates]
- Feel-Example-Draft §9b drive chunk: [if applicable — E117-E124]

**Research/documentation**:
- [Citations, memoirs, studies, documentaries]

**Framework insights**:
- [Key insight 1]
- [Key insight 2]

**Notes**:
- [Uncertainty, variation, counter-examples]
```

### §1.1 Case numbering

Use **B-series** (B1-B50) to distinguish from Feel-Example-Draft
E-series. "B" = Body-Base.

### §1.2 Case selection criteria

**Include**:
- Cases với clear channel dominance
- Cases với observable consequences
- Cases với documentation (memoirs, research, literature)
- Cross-cultural variety where possible
- Vietnamese cultural cases where relevant

**Exclude**:
- User's personal experience (NO PERSONAL INFO rule)
- Cases without clear channel mapping
- Speculation beyond evidence
- Confidential/private cases

### §1.3 Source types

**Primary sources**:
- Memoirs/autobiographies (Proenneke, Onoda, McCandless documented)
- Research case studies (published)
- Documentaries (Jiro Dreams of Sushi, Grizzly Man, etc.)
- Historical figures với documented lives
- General patterns (anonymized synthesis)

**Secondary sources**:
- Cultural observations
- Clinical literature
- Biographies

---

## §2 — WORK/ACHIEVEMENT EXTREMES (B1-B5)

### Category overview

Individuals với work/achievement channel dramatically over-fed,
thường kèm body, rest, nature, relational channels bị starved. Gồm
burnout cases, post-success emptiness cases, và một contrast case
về người duy trì balance bền vững. Category này đặc biệt quan
trọng bởi vì trong văn hóa modern (Mỹ, Nhật, Hàn, Trung, Việt),
work channel được cultural amplification mạnh — mức extreme trở
thành khá phổ biến.

### Channels this category primarily reveals

- **Achievement drive** (E118 obsessive inquiry, E119 legacy,
  E121 game — xem Feel-Example-Draft §9b) — chunks fire reward
  qua PFC, KHÔNG trực tiếp feed slow-decay body-base channels
- **Deep rest channel** (Body-Base.md §4.2.6) — distinct from
  sleep, thường là channel bị ignore nhất trong workaholic pattern
- **Movement + Nature channels** (§4.2.1, §4.2.2) — ngồi 70h/tuần
  trong văn phòng nhân tạo
- **Relational depth** (§4.2.3 agent) — quantity có (đồng nghiệp,
  meetings), quality không có (sâu, reciprocal, non-instrumental)
- **Meaning channel** (§4.3.3) — often discovered missing post-
  success, confirming achievement ≠ meaning

### Cross-reference (category-level)

- Feel-Example-Draft §9b: E118 (obsessive inquiry / nghiện), E119
  (legacy drive), E121 (game drive), E78 (feeling of knowing),
  E123 (craft mastery), E124 (meta-inquiry)
- Body-Base.md §4.3 higher-order channels (achievement as L2/L3
  compound), §4.2 silent channels (what gets starved)
- Body-Base.md §9 individual variation (why some burn out at 5
  năm, others last 20)
- Contrasting cases: B26 academic scholar (different channel
  compound), B36 fame seeker (status-driven vs work-driven)

---

### B1: Classic workaholic → burnout 🟡

**Scenario**:
Senior manager/professional, 40-55 tuổi, làm 70-90h/tuần liên tục
10-20 năm trong tech/finance/law/medicine. Pattern phổ biến: làm
muộn, check email ở nhà, weekend "just finish this", vacation
hủy hoặc làm việc từ xa, hobby ngày xưa bỏ dần, bạn bè non-work
mất liên lạc. Một ngày đột ngột (hoặc từ từ) "không thể làm
được nữa" — chronic fatigue, cynicism, mất lửa, đôi khi kèm
physical breakdown (cardiac event, autoimmune flare, chronic
back pain).

**Over-fed channel(s)**:
- **Primary — Achievement drive**: E118 obsessive inquiry + E119
  legacy + E121 game drive compound. Work task completion fires
  reward pattern tương đối reliably — PFC chunks activated, dopamine
  loop confirmed
- **Secondary — Identity channel**: self-concept progressively
  fused với role ("I am what I do" — Body-Base.md §9)
- **Tertiary — Social recognition**: colleagues, clients, status
  within organization — social reward present but narrow

**Starved channel(s)**:
- **Deep rest** (§4.2.6): không có chỗ trong lịch cho "doing
  nothing". Sleep có thể đủ giờ nhưng không phải deep rest (mind
  still running). Classic symptom: vacation đầu tiên sau nhiều
  năm = fall sick ngay ("leisure sickness" — Vingerhoets 2002)
- **Movement** (§4.2.1): desk-bound, chronic sedentary, posture
  chunks degraded, muscle atrophy trong key groups
- **Nature** (§4.2.2): weeks-months without outdoor exposure,
  circadian disruption, vitamin D deficit phổ biến
- **Agent-depth** (§4.2.3): quantity có (meetings, team) nhưng
  quality không — relationships instrumental, emotional
  reciprocity thấp
- **Touch** (§4.2.5): skin hunger phổ biến in single workaholics;
  even partnered ones often report "touch without being present"
- **Meaning** (§4.3.3): sometimes aligned với work, but often
  discovered deficient when "nếu tôi đã achieve X rồi thì sao?"

**Consequences observed**:
- Phase 1 (năm 1-5): high energy, identity reinforcement, "lửa"
  mạnh, PFC reward loop stable
- Phase 2 (năm 5-10): subtle degradation — "less fun", sleep
  quality decline, first GI/cardiac symptoms, snappiness ở nhà
- Phase 3 (năm 10-15): cynicism emerges (Maslach: "depersonal-
  ization"), sense of being "stuck", "mất lửa" begins intermittent
- Phase 4 (crash): sudden (panic attack, cardiac event) hoặc
  slow (depression, cannot get out of bed, "nothing matters
  anymore"). Recovery typically requires months-years, career
  often redirect
- Common physical manifestations: hypertension, IBS, autoimmune
  flares, chronic back/neck, cardiac events, sleep disorders

**Channel architecture revealed**:

Đây là case về **silent deficiency accumulation**. Achievement
channel fires reward reliably qua PFC — người workaholic KHÔNG
cảm thấy "đói" theo nghĩa loud-acute (không như đói bụng). Slow-
decay channels (rest, movement, nature, depth) suy thoái gradually,
melody slowly becomes dissonant. PFC không có vocabulary để diễn
tả các deficits này — "channel-lexithymia" (xem Body-Base.md §6).

Burnout endpoint reveals:
1. **Achievement chunks ≠ body-base channels**: firing PFC reward
   không thay thế được body-base slow-decay replenishment
2. **Silent channels can crash acutely**: khi multiple silent
   channels cùng starved đủ lâu, crash là sudden (not gradual
   warning)
3. **"Mất lửa" = meta-signal**: khi achievement channel itself
   mất khả năng fire reward, đó là body-base signal rằng
   supporting channels đã kiệt — body refuses to sustain the
   single-channel game anymore

**Cross-reference**:
- Similar cases: B2 billionaire (compound với status), B5 karoshi
  (cultural extreme), B26 academic scholar (different compound),
  B41 artist mania (creation instead of achievement)
- Contrasting: B4 balanced founder (demonstrates non-inevitability)
- Body-Base.md: §4.2.6 deep rest, §6 silent deficiency, §5 signal
  timeline model
- Feel-Example-Draft §9b: E118 obsessive inquiry as primary drive

**Research/documentation**:
- Maslach & Leiter (2016). "Understanding burnout syndrome."
  Current Opinion in Psychiatry 29(2). Three-dimensional model:
  exhaustion + cynicism + reduced efficacy
- Bianchi, Schonfeld & Laurent (2015). "Burnout-depression
  overlap." Clinical Psychology Review 36 — ~90% overlap
- Melamed et al. (2006). "Burnout and risk of cardiovascular
  disease." Psychological Bulletin 132(3) — prospective evidence
- Vingerhoets (2002). "Leisure sickness." Psychotherapy and
  Psychosomatics 71 — fall sick at start of vacation
- Pines & Keinan (2005). Burnout onset timing studies
- World Health Organization ICD-11 (2019) formal recognition of
  burnout as occupational phenomenon

**Framework insights**:
1. Burnout = **multi-channel silent deficit signal**, not single-
   channel crash. Framework predicts: recovery requires multi-
   channel restoration (rest + movement + nature + depth),
   not single intervention (e.g. just "more sleep")
2. **Achievement drive is PFC-intensive**: can sustain itself
   năm dài while body-base silently crashes, because reward
   firing doesn't require body-base input
3. **"Mất lửa" as clinical signal**: when achievement channel
   itself begins failing to fire (not because task failed but
   because body-base supporting system is depleted), the signal
   is valuable diagnostic — body refusing to run any further
   on empty
4. Validates Body-Base.md §5 **signal timeline model**: loud
   channels would give acute warning (fainting, collapse);
   silent channels accumulate silent deficit, then crash

**Notes**:
- High individual variation — some 5-năm crash, others 20+ năm.
  Factors: genetics (HPA axis resilience), sleep baseline, partial
  channel compensation (if has partner providing touch/depth, or
  commutes by walking, may last longer), personality (neuroticism
  accelerates)
- Recovery variable: some return to work after 6-12 months
  sabbatical; others need career change; small subset cannot
  fully recover cognitive capacity
- 🟡 confidence: pattern well-documented clinically, but specific
  channel architecture interpretation is framework synthesis

---

### B2: Billionaire post-success emptiness — Markus Persson pattern 🟢

**Scenario**:
Successful entrepreneur/founder achieves massive liquidity event
(sale, IPO). Financial goal fully attained. Within months,
reports unexpected emptiness, loss of purpose, sometimes severe
depression. Most public documented example: **Markus "Notch"
Persson** (Minecraft creator), who sold Minecraft to Microsoft
for $2.5 billion in 2014, then publicly tweeted in 2015:
"The problem with getting everything you ever wanted is that you
lose your reason to keep trying" and "Hanging out in Ibiza with
a bunch of friends and partying with famous people, able to do
whatever I want, and I've never felt more isolated."

Pattern phổ biến across self-made successful entrepreneurs —
documented in Dan Pink's "Drive", Tony Hsieh biography (tragic
end), multiple published founder interviews.

**Over-fed channel(s)**:
- **Achievement drive** (E118 + E121 game drive): entrepreneurial
  game was sustained primary channel 5-15 năm
- **Mastery channel** (§4.3.4): building/creating craft — real
  body-base adjacent reward during building phase
- **Status/recognition**: post-exit, social recognition at peak
- **Consumption capacity**: post-wealth, any material desire
  instantly fillable

**Starved channel(s)**:
- **Meaning channel** (§4.3.3): achievement-derived meaning
  collapses when achievement "complete" — meaning was borrowed
  from game, not independent
- **Agent-depth** (§4.2.3): post-wealth, relationships become
  suspect ("do they like me or the money?"), authentic reciprocity
  corrupted. Persson's "never felt more isolated" while partying
  with famous people = direct evidence of depth deficit despite
  quantity saturation
- **Novelty pursuit targets**: hedonic treadmill — any purchased
  novelty quickly normalized, reward degrades
- **Identity outside the game**: years of "I am the Minecraft
  guy / the founder" — post-exit, identity vacuum

**Consequences observed**:
- Immediate post-exit euphoria (weeks-months)
- Then: unexpected emptiness ("is this all?")
- Hedonic attempts (luxury consumption, parties, travel) fail to
  fill gap
- Often substance use, sometimes severe depression
- Recovery paths vary: some find philanthropy (meaning
  reconstruction), some return to building (new ventures),
  some spiritual/religious turn, some never recover well
- Markus Persson case: reports continuing struggle; public
  Twitter presence reflects ongoing difficulty years later

**Channel architecture revealed**:

Đây là case tinh khiết nhất về **achievement ≠ meaning** distinction.
Framework predicts: if meaning channel fed entirely qua achievement
game output, then goal completion = meaning channel immediately
empty. Persson's phenomenological report ("lose your reason to
keep trying") = direct evidence of meaning channel architecture
independent từ achievement channel.

Also reveals **relational-depth channel cannot be bought**:
unlimited financial resources did not produce depth relationships;
in fact wealth actively corrupted relational channel by making
reciprocity suspect. Channel has its own currency (vulnerability,
mutual dependence, time over years) that money cannot substitute.

Most high-signal: "never felt more isolated while surrounded by
famous people partying." Quantity maximum + quality zero = zero
fill. Channel is about **depth-not-quantity** — validates
Body-Base.md §4.2.3 spectrum (mere presence → observation →
interaction → deep bond).

**Cross-reference**:
- Similar cases: B36 fame seeker (social-based), B26 academic
  post-PhD (meaning collapse post-achievement), B3 Olympic gold
- Contrasting: B4 balanced founder (meaning constructed outside
  achievement), B27 Vietnamese craftsman (mastery channel without
  achievement endpoint)
- Body-Base.md: §4.3.3 meaning, §4.2.3 agent (depth spectrum),
  §4.3.4 mastery
- Feel-Example-Draft §9b: E118 obsessive inquiry, E119 legacy,
  E121 game drive

**Research/documentation**:
- Markus Persson public tweets (2015 onwards, documented in Kotaku,
  Vice, various tech press)
- Dan Pink (2009). "Drive: The Surprising Truth About What
  Motivates Us" — external reward insufficient thesis
- Kahneman & Deaton (2010). "High income improves evaluation
  of life but not emotional well-being." PNAS 107 — income
  threshold (~$75K) finding
- Ed Diener's hedonic adaptation research (extensive, 1984-)
- Tony Hsieh biography "Delivering Happiness" and subsequent
  reporting post-tragic death
- Bartels & Proietti (2017). "Sudden wealth syndrome."
  Financial Planning Review

**Framework insights**:
1. **Meaning channel is NOT downstream of achievement**: achievement
   can serve meaning if meaning comes from elsewhere (serving
   others, craft intrinsic, family legacy with real relationships),
   but achievement alone cannot generate meaning
2. **Relational depth is non-fungible**: cannot be purchased,
   upgraded, or accelerated. Has its own time-based currency
3. **Hedonic treadmill is architectural, not moral**: the
   problem isn't greed; the problem is that the novelty /
   acquisition channel decays faster than it can be refilled.
   Validates storage+decay model (Body-Base.md §7)
4. **Post-success emptiness = high-signal data** about which
   channels WERE being fed (the ones that feel stable) vs which
   were merely borrowed (the ones that collapse)

**Notes**:
- Not universal: many wealthy individuals avoid this pattern by
  having meaning-generating activities outside work, intact
  family relationships, philanthropy with real stakes, or simply
  personality structures less fused with achievement
- Distinction important: failure to feed meaning channel is
  NOT inevitable consequence of wealth; it's consequence of
  sustained single-channel overfeeding followed by channel
  termination
- 🟢 confidence: Persson case publicly documented via his own
  tweets; general pattern well-established across business
  psychology literature

---

### B3: Post-Olympic blues — Michael Phelps pattern 🟢

**Scenario**:
Elite athlete trains 15-25 năm với single-domain focus (swimming,
gymnastics, etc.), wins Olympic gold, then crashes into severe
depression within 3-12 months post-competition. **Michael Phelps**
publicly documented his post-2012 Olympics depression (HBO
documentary "The Weight of Gold" 2020 producer+participant);
**Allison Schmitt** similar testimony; **Ian Thorpe** depression
post-retirement; pattern repeated across sports (Olympic Committee
formally addresses post-Olympic depression since ~2016).

**Over-fed channel(s)**:
- **Achievement drive**: E118 obsessive inquiry compound với
  physical discipline 15+ năm, all hours of day organized around
  training
- **Mastery channel** (§4.3.4): extreme skill development feeds
  mastery reward reliably
- **Flow state** (§4.3.2): competition và training flow sessions
  frequent
- **Identity channel**: self-concept entirely fused với sport
  ("I am a swimmer")
- **Body engagement**: physical training daily, body channels
  well-fed during training years (movement, some nature if
  outdoor, rest via exhaustion)

**Starved channel(s)**:
- **Diversified identity**: single-channel identity structure —
  no "other" self
- **Meaning independent of sport**: entire meaning structure
  borrowed from competition goal
- **Relational depth outside sport context**: teammates present
  but bonds often transactional, non-sport friendships atrophied
- **Agency over own time**: every hour prescribed by coach/
  schedule, PFC decision-making channel atrophied
- **Post-peak purpose**: nothing exists beyond "next Olympics"

**Consequences observed**:
- Phelps: post-2004, post-2008, post-2012 all depressive episodes,
  suicidal ideation reported publicly ("didn't want to be
  alive" post-2012)
- Schmitt: severe depression, public advocacy post-recovery
- Thorpe: depression + alcohol, disclosed 2012
- Common pattern: 3-12 months post-competition, crash begins.
  "What now?" experience. Often first encounter with
  unstructured time. Identity vacuum
- Recovery paths: therapy, finding new purpose (coaching,
  advocacy, family), often new athletic pursuit (lesser but
  structured)

**Channel architecture revealed**:

Reveals **identity-channel fusion danger**: khi self-concept
entirely fused với single achievement channel, goal completion
= identity collapse. Framework insight: identity is not itself a
body-base channel, but rather a PFC structure mà body-base
channels feed INTO. Single-source feeding = fragile structure.

Also distinct from B2 billionaire case because: during training
years, body channels (movement, rest-via-exhaustion, flow) were
well-fed. Post-competition, these too suddenly dry up — not just
meaning collapses, but physical body-base routine that sustained
mental stability also dissolves. Triple collapse: achievement
complete + identity vacuum + body-base routine ceased.

**"What now?" phenomenology**: the question is not rhetorical —
it's a direct verbalization của meaning channel discovering it
has no independent input source. PFC forced to face the silent
deficit that training structure was masking.

**Cross-reference**:
- Similar cases: B2 billionaire, B26 post-PhD academic,
  B36 fame seeker, B42 performance obsession
- Contrasting: B10 ultra-marathon (continued engagement), B27
  craftsman (no endpoint, ongoing channel)
- Body-Base.md: §4.3 higher-order channels, §4.2.1 movement,
  §4.2.6 deep rest, §9 individual variation
- Feel-Example-Draft §9b: E122 flow, E123 craft mastery, E121
  game drive

**Research/documentation**:
- Howells & Lucassen (2018). "Post-Olympic blues: exploring
  experiences of elite athletes." Psychology of Sport and
  Exercise 37
- "The Weight of Gold" (HBO 2020, Phelps executive producer)
- US Olympic Committee mental health task force (2018+)
- International Olympic Committee Consensus Statement on Mental
  Health (2019)
- Schinke et al. (2018). "Athletes' mental health." Int Review
  of Sport and Exercise Psychology

**Framework insights**:
1. **Identity-channel fusion is fragility, not strength**: the
   athlete who "gives everything to the sport" is structurally
   more vulnerable, not more committed. Framework implication:
   healthy development = multi-channel identity diversification,
   not single-channel intensification
2. **Body-base routines mask silent deficits**: structured
   training schedule provides forced multi-channel input
   (movement, rest, flow, purpose), hiding the deficit until
   routine ends. Cessation reveals accumulated non-channels
3. **Goal-completion = potential crash trigger**: achievement
   chunks complete and derecruit, leaving void. Individuals
   with external-to-sport channels (family, academic pursuits,
   faith, other craft) weather this better — validated by
   athletes who retired well vs those who crashed

**Notes**:
- Not all elite athletes crash — those who maintained parallel
  channels (education, family, non-sport friends, spiritual
  practice) typically weather transition better
- Gender patterns: documented in both male and female athletes;
  severity similar, disclosure rates differ culturally
- Early specialization (childhood) correlates with worse
  transition outcomes — fewer opportunities for parallel
  channel development during developmental years. Relevant to
  Child-Development framework files
- 🟢 confidence: publicly documented, research-supported pattern

---

### B4: Balanced founder — contrast case 🟡

**Scenario**:
Founder/CEO/senior leader who maintains sustainable multi-channel
life across 20-30+ năm career: work 45-55 hours (not 80+),
protected family time, daily exercise, sleep discipline, ongoing
friendships outside work, often a non-work practice (meditation,
music, craft, faith). Examples loosely associated with this
pattern in public discourse: **Satya Nadella** (Microsoft CEO,
meditation, family boundaries, writing), **Jeff Weiner** (former
LinkedIn CEO, meditation advocate, compassionate leadership
frame), **Tim Cook** (disciplined routine, long-sustained), và
many less-famous founders documented in business press.

Cần làm rõ: contrast case không phải "less ambitious" — these
leaders achieved comparable or higher outcomes than burnout cases.
Contrast variable = multi-channel maintenance, not lowered drive.

**Over-fed channel(s)**:
- **Achievement drive** (moderate): present but not monopolizing
- **Mastery channel**: well-fed via deep work in focused blocks
- **Meaning channel** (§4.3.3): typically well-constructed —
  mission orientation, service framing, generational thinking
- **Agent-depth** (§4.2.3): protected spousal/family relationships,
  sustained close friendships
- **Deep rest** (§4.2.6): disciplined — meditation, reading, sleep
  hygiene, vacation taken seriously
- **Movement + nature** (partial): daily exercise, often outdoor

**Starved channel(s)**:
- None chronically. May have seasonal strain (product launch,
  crisis), but return to baseline
- Occasional thin periods in specific sub-channels (e.g. extended
  travel reducing nature access) compensated elsewhere

**Consequences observed**:
- Sustainable over 20+ năm — career longevity high
- Continued cognitive sharpness into 60s
- Intact family relationships (partner, children grown healthy)
- Physical health generally maintained (age-appropriate)
- Lower incidence of sudden health events
- **Crucially**: comparable or superior achievement outcomes
  vs burnout peers — not "less ambitious" but "differently
  structured"
- Typical trajectory: 20-30 năm leadership, then often transition
  to advisory/board/teaching/philanthropy — phased rather than
  crash

**Channel architecture revealed**:

**Burnout is NOT inevitable consequence of ambition** — it is
consequence of single-channel dominance. This case demonstrates
that ambition at highest levels is compatible with multi-channel
maintenance given deliberate construction. Framework claim: the
crash risk variable is channel architecture, not intensity.

Also reveals **protective factors**:
1. **Early deliberate construction**: almost all sustained cases
   established boundaries BEFORE peak career pressure. Trying to
   construct boundaries once already caught in workaholic spiral
   is structurally much harder
2. **Partner/family as anchor**: spousal relationships consistently
   feature in sustained cases — providing forced non-work channel
   input (conversation, touch, mundane presence)
3. **Practice outside work**: meditation, music, sport — provides
   non-achievement channel fire pattern, breaking exclusive
   work-reward loop
4. **Identity not fused**: self-concept includes non-work
   dimensions — "I am a parent, musician, reader, friend" alongside
   role

**Cross-reference**:
- Contrasting cases: B1 workaholic, B2 billionaire empty, B3
  Olympic, B5 karoshi — all single-channel dominance
- Body-Base.md: §4.3 higher-order channels, §9 individual
  variation, §13 integration principles
- Feel-Example-Draft §9b: all drive chunks present but in
  moderation — E117-E124 compound

**Research/documentation**:
- Satya Nadella (2017). "Hit Refresh." Memoir describing multi-
  channel life and leadership philosophy
- Jeff Weiner public talks and interviews on meditation, family
  boundaries (LinkedIn, various)
- Harvard Business Review "Sustainable Leadership" literature
  (Boyatzis et al., 2006+)
- Grant & Schwartz (2011). "Too much of a good thing: The
  challenge and opportunity of the inverted U." Perspectives on
  Psychological Science 6(1) — diminishing returns thesis
- Literature on resilience in leadership (George Kohlrieser,
  Bruce Avolio, etc.)

**Framework insights**:
1. **Contrast case is framework-critical**: burnout cases alone
   might suggest "achievement = body-base killer." Contrast
   cases refute this and isolate the actual variable — channel
   monopolization, not channel use
2. **Multi-channel maintenance requires deliberate construction**:
   default drift in high-pressure careers IS toward monopolization.
   Balance is active, not passive. Framework implication:
   protective structures must be installed early và defended
3. **Sustainability = multi-source feeding**: achievement
   channel can remain intensely active if OTHER channels also
   remain fed. Total system energy is not "zero-sum" because
   channels are substrate-independent
4. **Validates Body-Base.md §13**: healthy operation = multiple
   channels fed; pathology = monopoly or starvation

**Notes**:
- Difficult to document cleanly because success stories get
  less journalistic coverage than crashes (survivorship/selection
  bias). Balanced people working sustainably are "boring" news
- Individual variation: some personalities find balance easier
  (secure attachment, lower neuroticism), others require more
  deliberate construction. Not a character judgment — an
  architectural observation
- Cultural note: American founder culture often rewards
  monopolization rhetorically ("hustle porn"), even while
  sustained leaders practice otherwise. Public narrative
  mismatches actual sustainable practice
- 🟡 confidence: pattern observable across successful long-
  career leaders, but specific framework interpretation is
  synthesis

---

### B5: Karoshi — Japanese death by overwork 🟢

**Scenario**:
Japanese salaryman (typically male, 30-50s, white-collar), 80-
110 hours/week over 20-40 năm trong cultural environment where
leaving before the boss is socially impossible. Sudden death from
cardiovascular event (stroke, cardiac arrest), or suicide from
depression (**karōjisatsu**). Japanese government officially
recognizes karoshi since 1987; Ministry of Health & Labour
annual reports document cases. Formally: death certified as
karoshi when overtime exceeds ~80-100 hours/month for months
preceding cardiovascular event, or depression leading to suicide
clearly work-caused.

Notable public cases: **Matsuri Takahashi** (Dentsu, suicide 2015
age 24, triggered national reform); multiple documented cases
in Dentsu, Toyota, various trading firms; 2016 White Paper on
Karoshi formal government publication.

Related: Korean "gwarosa", Chinese "guolaosi" — similar patterns,
same mechanism.

**Over-fed channel(s)**:
- **Work quantity (not drive)** — critical distinction from B1:
  Japanese workaholic pattern often NOT passion-driven; it is
  PRESSURE-driven. Group belonging + face + cultural expectation
  force presence, not internal game drive
- **Group belonging compound**: social belonging channel activated
  through forced group presence — but through fear of exclusion,
  not positive reward
- **Achievement (secondary)**: present but often subordinate to
  group pressure

**Starved channel(s)**:
- **Sleep** (§4.1.5): chronically <5 giờ, sometimes <4 giờ. THIS
  is acute-channel starvation, cardinal difference from B1
  which usually maintains minimum sleep
- **Deep rest** (§4.2.6): zero
- **Movement** (§4.2.1): desk-bound + office sedentary culture
- **Nature** (§4.2.2): commute dark-to-dark, buildings never
  leaving
- **Agent-depth** (§4.2.3): wife/family seen rarely (children
  grown up seeing father briefly weekends), friendships non-
  existent outside work
- **Touch** (§4.2.5): chronic skin hunger
- **Meaning** (§4.3.3): complicated — some find meaning in
  company loyalty; many do not. Where meaning absent AND all
  other channels starved = suicide risk elevated

**Consequences observed**:
- Cardiovascular event risk sharply elevated: stroke, myocardial
  infarction, cerebral hemorrhage
- Sudden cardiac death in 30s-50s unusual demographic
- Severe depression, with Takahashi-type suicide trajectory
- Chronic health conditions (hypertension, diabetes, metabolic
  syndrome) prevalent among survivors
- Family consequences: absentee parenting, generational
  transmission of pattern, high divorce
- Suicide by specific method pattern documented (jumping from
  workplace, hanging)

**Channel architecture revealed**:

Đây là case về **cultural amplification of single-channel
dominance WITHOUT individual drive**. Distinguishes from B1
(passion workaholic) critically: in B1, individual drive over-
feeds achievement channel; in B5, cultural pressure forces
single-channel presence regardless of individual drive. Same
channel architecture consequence (everything else starves), but
different originating mechanism.

Second key insight: **when ALL body-base channels simultaneously
starved AND one acute channel (sleep) is also starved, the
combined deficit produces ACUTE crash** (cardiovascular death),
not just slow decay. Usually silent channels crash slowly; but
combined with sleep deprivation + chronic stress + no movement
+ no recovery, the system can break acutely within years.
Validates Body-Base.md §5 signal timeline model but extends:
simultaneous multi-channel deprivation can compress timelines.

Third: **group belonging activated by fear is not nourishing**.
Social channel requires positive reciprocity; fear-based group
presence consumes, not feeds. This refines Body-Base.md §4.2.3:
agent channel has quality dimension, not just quantity.

**Cross-reference**:
- Similar cases: B1 workaholic (passion-driven version), B14
  Vietnamese family obligation (cultural counterpart different
  channel), B22 cult member (group pressure counterpart)
- Contrasting: B4 balanced founder
- Body-Base.md: §4.1.5 sleep, §4.2.3 agent quality spectrum,
  §4.2.6 deep rest, §5 signal timeline, §10 cultural variation
- Feel-Example-Draft: E18 shame/group, E49 shame chunks,
  §9b compound drive chunks absence (pressure-driven is
  distinct)

**Research/documentation**:
- Nishiyama & Johnson (1997). "Karoshi — Death from overwork:
  occupational health consequences of Japanese production
  management." International Journal of Health Services 27(4)
- Iwasaki, Takahashi & Nakata (2006). "Health problems due to
  long working hours in Japan: working hours, workers'
  compensation (Karoshi), and preventive measures." Industrial
  Health 44
- Japanese Ministry of Health, Labour and Welfare. "White Paper
  on Measures to Prevent Karoshi" (annual since 2016)
- Kanai (2009). "'Karoshi (Work to Death)' in Japan." Journal
  of Business Ethics 84
- North & Morioka (2016). "Hope found in lives lost: Karoshi
  and the pursuit of worker rights in Japan." Contemporary
  Japan 28(1) — Takahashi case
- Park et al. (2012) — Korean gwarosa parallel research

**Framework insights**:
1. **Culture can force channel architecture without individual
   volition**: Framework must distinguish *voluntary* single-
   channel dominance (B1) from *involuntary* (B5). Both produce
   similar body-base outcomes but require different interventions
2. **Fear-based social presence is not body-base-fulfilling**:
   agent channel quality dimension is load-bearing. Being
   physically present in group while fearing exclusion does NOT
   replenish agent channel; it may even deplete
3. **Simultaneous multi-channel deprivation compresses timeline**:
   when silent + acute channels all starve together, "silent"
   decay becomes acute crash. Framework refinement: §5 signal
   timeline assumes some channels maintained — worst case
   compounds differently
4. **Cultural intervention is structural intervention**: Japan's
   gradual labor law reform (work hour caps post-2017 Takahashi
   response) shows systemic problems need systemic fixes.
   Individual advice ("take care of yourself") fails against
   cultural force
5. **Validates meaning channel importance**: karōjisatsu
   (depression suicide) more common among workers who also
   lacked meaning; pure cardiovascular karoshi sometimes
   affected those who had meaning but just body crashed. Meaning
   and body channels are semi-separable in outcomes

**Notes**:
- Korean gwarosa and Chinese guolaosi parallel patterns — same
  mechanism, same cultural amplification, documented across
  East Asian industrial economies
- Vietnamese emerging parallel in recent decades as work culture
  intensifies; worth watching as cultural variant
- Western "hustle culture" creates similar pressure but with
  more individual opt-out possibility and weaker group face
  mechanism — produces B1 pattern more than B5
- Interesting gender note: karoshi classically male (salaryman);
  Takahashi case (female, young, advertising industry) signaled
  pattern extending to younger women — cultural shift
- 🟢 confidence: government-documented, research-substantiated

---

## §3 — NATURE/MOVEMENT EXTREMES (B6-B10)

### Category overview

Individuals dramatically invested vào nature/movement channels,
either by choice (digital nomad, extreme athlete) or by
circumstance/tradition (homesteader, farmer). Unlike Work/
Achievement category nơi silent channels bị starved, Nature/
Movement category cases show **silent channels in abundance** —
revealing what these channels actually provide khi được fed
at high dose, and which OTHER channels they cannot substitute.

Category đặc biệt critical cho framework vì nó validates directly
framework's claim về silent/slow-decay channels: if nature,
movement, và living pattern channels weren't real body-base
needs, sustained high-dose engagement wouldn't produce distinctive
positive outcomes nor reveal distinctive boundary problems.

### Channels this category primarily reveals

- **Movement channel** (§4.2.1) — what high-dose physical activity
  provides (flow access, endorphin loop, body integrity signals,
  circadian regulation)
- **Nature channel** (§4.2.2) — what sustained natural environment
  exposure provides (sensory richness, fractal engagement, air/
  light/temperature calibration, phytoncides)
- **Living pattern channel** (§4.2.4) — often over-fed alongside
  nature (wildlife, plants moving, seasonal cycles visible)
- **Flow state** (§4.3.2) — frequently compound in this category
- **Adventure/novelty** (L2 compound) — travel nomads especially
- **What these channels DO NOT substitute**: relational depth
  (often starved), meaning independent of movement, community
  embeddedness, specialized skill accumulation (for mobile cases)

### Cross-reference (category-level)

- Body-Base.md: §4.2.1 movement, §4.2.2 nature, §4.2.4 living
  pattern, §4.3.2 flow
- Feel-Example-Draft §9b: E117 curiosity drive, E122 flow state,
  E123 craft (homesteader compound)
- Calibration-Inputs-Analysis.md research foundation (Biophilia,
  Forest bathing, Attention Restoration — will be absorbed into
  Body-Base.md §4.2.2)
- Contrasting categories: §2 Work/Achievement (nature starved),
  §8 Consumption (different compound)

---

### B6: Digital nomad 10+ năm — the "endless travel" pattern 🟡

**Scenario**:
Individual (often 25-45 tuổi) who quits settled life và spends
10+ năm traveling continuously — van life, country hopping,
remote work from different city monthly, or retirement-age
continuous RV travel. Pattern involves high nature exposure
(national parks, landscapes, outdoor life), high movement
(hiking, swimming, cycling, walking new cities daily), high
novelty (new environments constantly). Documented publicly via
countless travel blogs, YouTube channels, van life communities,
và memoirs such as Rolf Potts' "Vagabonding" (2003).

Critical observation: community forums and long-tail blog
confessionals document a recurring **burnout pattern** emerging
around năm 7-12 for most sustained nomads — suddenly "travel
fatigue", emptiness, inability to enjoy new places, sometimes
depression, often precipitating return to settled life.

**Over-fed channel(s)**:
- **Nature** (§4.2.2): constant outdoor exposure, varied
  environments, sensory richness maximum
- **Movement** (§4.2.1): daily walking, hiking, swimming —
  movement channel well-fed in naturalistic way (not gym
  artificial)
- **Novelty** (L2 compound): every location new, every vista
  novel, dopamine novelty system chronically activated
- **Autonomy/agency** (PFC channel): unusual degree of schedule
  self-determination
- **Light agent breadth**: constant new surface relationships,
  travelers met, locals briefly encountered

**Starved channel(s)**:
- **Relational depth** (§4.2.3): acute starvation. Depth requires
  sustained presence over years với same individuals. Nomadic
  pattern structurally precludes this. Quantity high (many
  encounters) but quality ceiling low (weeks-max). Surface
  connections feel nourishing initially but accumulate deficit
  — "everyone I care about is far away"
- **Living pattern embedded** (§4.2.4 paradox): ironically, despite
  being in natural environments với much living pattern, the
  nomad is NEVER embedded IN any one living pattern long enough
  to experience the channel that comes from *belonging* to a
  domain. Watching life move in a place where you've been 3 weeks
  is different from watching life move in a place where you've
  been 10 năm — the second is body-base richer
- **Meaning stability** (§4.3.3): novelty-driven meaning decays;
  sustained meaning requires commitment to something (people,
  project, place, craft)
- **Mastery/skill accumulation** (§4.3.4): mobile lifestyle
  limits depth skill investment; breadth high, depth low
- **Community membership**: not just relationships but being
  *recognized, expected, missed* by a group — nomads rarely
  experience

**Consequences observed**:
- Phase 1 (năm 1-3): peak euphoria, nature + movement + novelty
  compound fires strongly, often experienced as "best years
  of life"
- Phase 2 (năm 3-7): continued high functioning, but beginning
  "the quiet question" — sometimes suppressed. "What am I
  building?"
- Phase 3 (năm 7-12): travel fatigue emerges — new locations
  less exciting, novelty adaptation complete, "I've seen
  enough mountains." Relational loneliness breaking through
  often. Some crash into depression; others pivot
- Common pivot patterns: (1) return to settled life entirely,
  often with "why did I wait so long" regret, (2) partial
  settlement với kept travel component, (3) rare sustained
  nomads who typically have strong family bond traveling with
  them (reducing relational deficit)
- Common recovery: finding a place + community + project =
  rapid settling, as if body-base channels were waiting for
  substrate

**Channel architecture revealed**:

Đây là case critical cho framework vì nó demonstrates **nature +
movement channel over-feeding DOES NOT substitute relational
depth channel**. The nomad has maximum nature input yet eventually
crashes on relational deficit — proves these are architecturally
separate channels, không phải fungible aspects of "outdoor life".

Also reveals **embeddedness as distinct from exposure**: watching
wildlife in a place you'll leave in 3 weeks is different from
watching wildlife in a place you've been 10 năm. Embedded
living pattern channel seems to require commitment dimension
that mere exposure doesn't provide — refines Body-Base.md §4.2.4
living pattern channel. Proposed framework refinement: living
pattern channel has *exposure* sub-component (feeds quickly,
saturates) và *belonging* sub-component (feeds only with
sustained membership).

**Novelty adaptation hit**: novelty-feeding channel DOES decay
và adapt. Even maximum novelty input cannot sustain novelty
feeding indefinitely — dopaminergic adaptation is inescapable.
Framework implication: novelty pursuit strategies are
architecturally limited, cannot replace channels that don't
adapt (like meaning, depth relationships).

**"Rollover" to settled life recovery speed**: the rapidity
với which ex-nomads report settling (often weeks-months to
feel "finally home") suggests the starved channels were
waiting for opportunity — channel deficit is reversible when
substrate becomes available. Validates framework claim that
body-base channels have resilient restoration capacity given
proper inputs.

**Cross-reference**:
- Similar cases: B8 homesteader (sustained but embedded), B10
  ultra-marathon (movement extreme without nomadic), B6 vs
  contrasting B26 academic (opposite: embedded + sedentary)
- Contrasting: B9 farmer (maximum embeddedness), B4 balanced
  founder (settled với multi-channel)
- Body-Base.md: §4.2.2 nature, §4.2.4 living pattern
  (embedded vs exposure distinction), §4.2.3 agent depth
- Feel-Example-Draft §9b: E117 curiosity (often primary drive),
  E122 flow in new environments

**Research/documentation**:
- Rolf Potts (2003). "Vagabonding: An Uncommon Guide to the
  Art of Long-Term World Travel" — foundational text, later
  "Vagabonding Cafe" community discussions document burnout
- Nomadic Matt Kepnes blogs — 10+ năm documentation including
  mid-career settling reconsideration
- Digital nomad community surveys (Nomad List, various)
- Academic: Reichenberger (2018). "Digital nomads — a quest
  for holistic freedom in work and leisure." Annals of Leisure
  Research 21(3)
- Thompson (2019). "The digital nomad lifestyle: (remote) work/
  leisure balance, privilege, and constructed community."
  International Journal of the Sociology of Leisure 2
- Memoir literature: "A Year to Live Abroad" genre, "How to
  Travel Forever" confessionals

**Framework insights**:
1. **Nature abundance ≠ relational substitute**: architecturally
   separate channels. Sustained nomad cases definitively refute
   substitution hypothesis
2. **Novelty-fed channels have adaptation ceiling**: dopaminergic
   novelty cannot indefinitely feed; framework must account for
   adaptation as architectural feature
3. **Embeddedness is distinct channel variable**: exposure to
   nature/living pattern in a place you belong is different
   from exposure to nature/living pattern in a place you're
   passing through. Framework proposal: add embeddedness as
   dimension within §4.2.4 living pattern
4. **Restoration capacity high**: ex-nomads recovering within
   weeks of settling suggests channel deficits are resilient
   to reversal, not permanent damage. Good news for framework
   recovery predictions
5. **Age interaction**: young nomads (20s) can sustain longer
   before crash (less existing commitment to miss); mid-life
   (30s-40s) tend to crash faster when loneliness or "what
   am I building" emerges

**Notes**:
- Subset of nomads avoid crash by traveling với partner/family —
  reduces relational deficit significantly. Family nomads
  sometimes sustain 20+ năm
- Retirement-age RV nomads different pattern: shorter absolute
  duration, lower channel stakes (existing relationships settled)
- Work-integrated digital nomads (consistent remote job, not
  "free") tend to have faster recovery because one anchor
  channel remained throughout
- 🟡 confidence: pattern documented in community literature
  và emerging academic research, but clean longitudinal data
  scarce

---

### B7: Extreme sports athlete — free solo climber pattern 🟢

**Scenario**:
Individual dedicates life to extreme sport với mortality risk:
free solo climbing (no rope), big wave surfing, alpinism, base
jumping, wingsuit flying. **Alex Honnold** (Free Solo 2018, El
Capitan no rope) is most publicly documented case. **Dean Potter**
(died 2015 BASE jumping Yosemite), **Ueli Steck** (died 2017
Nuptse), **Dan Osman** (died 1998 rope jumping), **Shane
McConkey** (died 2009 wingsuit) represent the pattern's fatal
outcomes. **Timothy Treadwell** (Werner Herzog's "Grizzly Man"
2005) represents romantic/spiritual wilderness immersion pattern
ending fatally (killed by bear 2003).

Notable research: neuroscientist Jane Joseph scanned Alex
Honnold's amygdala (2016) và found unusually low reactivity
to fearful stimuli — published in Nautilus magazine, generated
scientific community discussion.

**Over-fed channel(s)**:
- **Flow state** (§4.3.2): this category arguably achieves
  most intense flow of any human activity — life-and-death
  absolute focus, no mental space for anything else, hours-
  long uninterrupted flow sessions
- **Mastery** (§4.3.4): decades of specific skill accumulation,
  mastery compound với flow — reward system heavily activated
- **Nature exposure** (§4.2.2): wilderness, mountains, ocean
  — typically sustained natural environment
- **Movement** (§4.2.1): peak physical training required
- **Meaning** (§4.3.3): often philosophical/spiritual dimension,
  "why I climb" as identity integration

**Starved channel(s)**:
- **Safety channel** (§4.1.6): fundamentally starved by design.
  Every session = high mortality risk. This channel architecturally
  CANNOT be fed while pursuing activity
- **Relational depth** (§4.2.3): heavily compromised. Partners,
  parents, children often bear cost of watching — many public
  cases include partners' testimony of terror. High fatality
  rates mean bereavement in community constant
- **Longevity** (meta-channel): median age at death in extreme
  alpine climbing estimated 35-45, BASE jumping similar

**Consequences observed**:
- Sustained practitioners: extraordinary flow access, reported
  "most alive" phenomenology, decades of peak experiences
- **Mortality**: ~1% per year in extreme alpinism (climbing
  deaths database studies); BASE jumping ~1% per year
  approximate. Cumulative risk over 20 năm career: significant
  fraction do not survive
- **Survivor pattern**: those who retire alive (Honnold has
  partially transitioned to film/family) report profound
  reconciliation challenges — "nothing else compares"
- **Grief distribution**: entire community carries accumulated
  bereavement; documentary "Meru" shows this
- Treadwell specific: 13 năm summer bear coexistence, boundary
  erosion, fatal outcome 2003

**Channel architecture revealed**:

Reveals **flow state as powerful standalone channel**. Free
solo flow sessions documented to produce states phenomenologically
describable as transcendent, time-dilated, ego-dissolved — the
strongest flow evidence outside meditation literature. Framework
insight: flow channel can be pursued even at lethal cost,
suggesting exceptional reward intensity.

Also reveals **safety channel is body-base architectural floor**,
not optional. Practitioners don't eliminate fear — they bypass it
(Honnold low amygdala reactivity) or integrate it (other climbers
report fear as "partner"). But the body-base safety system
remains operating; it simply cannot mount effective refusal in
these individuals.

**Trade-off pattern**: maximum flow access purchased at cost of
lifespan. Framework implication: channels can trade against
each other, but some trades are catastrophic. Extreme sports =
flow-for-longevity trade. Validates "no channel fully substitutes
another" AND shows trades are possible at existential cost.

**Amygdala research significance**: Honnold specifically shows
neural basis of reduced fear response. Suggests individual
variation in safety channel calibration — some people architecturally
"wired" for reduced threat response. Does NOT mean others can
learn this — the variation may be trait-level.

**Treadwell boundary erosion**: 13 năm of escalating wilderness
immersion losing distinction between "observer of nature" and
"participant in nature" — the fatal error was boundary loss
with apex predator. Framework interpretation: nature channel
feeding can produce immersion so intense that PFC safety
channel monitoring is overridden. Not pure nature channel
goodness — nature channel has its own risk profile when
over-fed without PFC restraint.

**Cross-reference**:
- Similar cases: B10 ultra-marathon (sub-lethal intensity),
  B3 Olympic (mastery + flow compound, not lethal)
- Contrasting: B9 farmer (nature sustained without risk),
  B4 balanced founder (flow access without lethality)
- Body-Base.md: §4.3.2 flow, §4.1.6 safety (as architectural
  floor), §9 individual variation (amygdala findings)
- Feel-Example-Draft §9b: E122 flow, E117 curiosity (extreme
  variant)

**Research/documentation**:
- Joseph (2016). Alex Honnold amygdala fMRI study. Popular
  science coverage: Nautilus magazine "The Strange Brain of
  the World's Greatest Solo Climber" by J.B. MacKinnon
- "Free Solo" (National Geographic 2018, Oscar 2019) —
  Chin & Vasarhelyi
- "Meru" (2015) — climbing + relationships documentary
- "Grizzly Man" (Werner Herzog 2005) — Treadwell
- Climbing mortality statistics: American Alpine Club
  "Accidents in North American Climbing" (annual)
- Westmacott (1995). "Sports and exercise psychology: extreme
  sport motivation research"
- Willig (2008). "A phenomenological investigation of the
  experience of taking part in 'extreme sports'." Journal
  of Health Psychology 13(5)
- Brymer & Schweitzer (2013). "Extreme sports are good for
  your health: A phenomenological understanding of fear and
  anxiety in extreme sport." Journal of Health Psychology
  18(4)

**Framework insights**:
1. **Flow channel can be extraordinarily rewarding**: its pursuit
   at lethal risk validates framework ranking of flow as
   major body-base-adjacent channel
2. **Channels can trade catastrophically**: flow ↔ longevity
   trade is documented. Framework must account for trade-off
   architecture, not just individual channel needs
3. **Safety channel as architectural floor**: cannot be truly
   eliminated — only bypassed or numbed. Individual variation
   (Honnold amygdala) exists at trait level
4. **Nature channel has dark side**: over-immersion without
   PFC restraint (Treadwell) can cross safety boundary.
   Channel is not uniformly positive — dose and boundary matter
5. **Community bereavement as channel cost**: extreme sports
   communities carry accumulated grief — this cost is often
   invisible in individual analysis but real at community level

**Notes**:
- Gender pattern: extreme sports demographic skews heavily
  male; risk tolerance and identity variables suggested but
  not fully explained
- Distinction between calculated-risk extreme sports (alpinism
  với systems) và raw extreme (free solo, BASE) — mortality
  rates different, phenomenology similar
- Age progression: practitioners often retire by 40s-50s
  voluntarily or forcibly (injury, fatality of close friends,
  family formation). Sustained beyond 50 unusual
- 🟢 confidence: well-documented research, films, mortality
  statistics, phenomenological literature

---

### B8: Homesteader / back-to-land — multi-channel restoration 🟡

**Scenario**:
Urban/suburban professional (often 30-50 tuổi) quits city life,
moves to rural property, builds/renovates, grows food, often
raises family, 20+ năm sustained. Pattern includes: physical
labor daily, nature exposure constant, building/repairing/craft
work, children growing up embedded in landscape, community
participation in small town, often homeschooling or small
school. Not "retreat from civilization" so much as "construction
of different civilization architecture".

Literary/documentary tradition: **Helen & Scott Nearing**
"Living the Good Life" (1954) documented 60+ năm homesteading;
**Wendell Berry** (farmer-poet-philosopher, Kentucky, 50+ năm)
documents sustained agrarian life; modern homesteading
movement well-represented in YouTube (Justin Rhodes, Roots and
Refuge, Homesteady), memoirs (Jenna Woginrich "Barnheart"),
và academic tradition.

Distinguished from B9 (farmer) by typical origin: homesteaders
choose rural life from non-rural background, making it a
deliberate construction; B9 farmers are often born into
agricultural life.

**Over-fed channel(s)**:
- **Nature** (§4.2.2): daily outdoor, seasonal exposure, weather
  immersion, soil contact
- **Movement** (§4.2.1): hauling, digging, carrying, chopping
  — varied physical work, not repetitive exercise
- **Living pattern** (§4.2.4 embedded): watching animals, plants,
  seasons, other families within community — embedded version
  of channel, not mere exposure
- **Mastery** (§4.3.4): diverse practical skills compound (carpen-
  try, gardening, animal husbandry, food preservation, repair) —
  breadth and depth both present
- **Meaning** (§4.3.3): typically strong construction —
  providing for family, connecting to land, multi-generational
  building, often faith component
- **Family depth**: children grow up embedded in daily parental
  life (unusual in industrial societies)
- **Touch** (§4.2.5): soil, animals, children, partner —
  sustained daily contact with physical world and people
- **Silence** (§4.2.8): rural soundscape, nights genuinely
  dark and quiet

**Starved channel(s)**:
- **Specialized achievement reward**: if ambitious by
  conventional metrics, this pattern doesn't feed that. Voluntarily
  starved for most homesteaders
- **External novelty**: less "new thing" stimulation, though
  seasonal variation provides some
- **Intellectual depth**: variable — some homesteaders maintain
  voracious reading/writing (Wendell Berry), others let this
  channel dim
- **Economic stability**: real risk — small agriculture
  frequently economically marginal. Stress channel sometimes
  activated over finances

**Consequences observed**:
- **Low burnout rate**: sustained cases report sustained
  satisfaction. Not euphoric but stable
- **Physical toll**: joint wear, back injuries, sun damage
  — real but distributed over years, rarely acute
- **Cognitive preservation**: anecdotally, homesteaders
  cognitively sharp into 80s-90s (Nearings both productive
  into 90s); no longitudinal research confirms
- **Economic strain common**: most supplement với off-farm
  income, teaching, writing, seasonal work
- **Drop-out pattern**: subset do return to urban life
  (~20-30% within first 5 năm), typically due to: economic
  unviability, social isolation for one partner, underestimation
  of physical demands, or children's education concerns
- **Multi-generational**: sustained homesteads often become
  family traditions spanning 2-3 generations

**Channel architecture revealed**:

Đây là case về **multi-channel restoration** — nhiều silent
channels simultaneously fed at moderate sustained dose. Contrast
sharp với B6 nomad (nature + movement over-fed, relational
starved) and B1 workaholic (achievement over-fed, everything
else starved): homesteader distributes inputs across channels
instead of concentrating.

Reveals **sustainability signature**: channels fed at moderate
sustained dose are more sustainable than high-intensity single-
channel approaches. Framework refinement: peak channel intensity
is NOT the goal; multi-channel baseline presence is. Validates
Body-Base.md §13 integration framework — thriving = multi-channel
operation, not maximum single-channel.

Also reveals **embeddedness as channel feeder**: unlike nomad
(exposure high, embeddedness zero), homesteader has high
embeddedness — same land, same animals, same neighbors over
decades. Embeddedness feeds living pattern, community, và
meaning channels simultaneously in ways exposure cannot.

**Voluntary starvation of achievement channel**: homesteaders
typically sacrifice conventional achievement metrics. Framework
insight: this channel is trainable down — lower demand if
replaced with mastery + meaning + family. Not all channels
require saturation; some can be downregulated if others fed.

**Cross-reference**:
- Similar cases: B9 farmer (born-to version), B27 craftsman
  (mastery compound), B14 Vietnamese extended family (community
  embeddedness parallel)
- Contrasting: B6 nomad (exposure without embeddedness), B1
  workaholic (opposite channel allocation), B2 billionaire
  empty (achievement-rich/meaning-poor opposite pattern)
- Body-Base.md: §4.2 silent channels broadly, §4.3.4 mastery,
  §4.3.3 meaning, §13 integration principles
- Feel-Example-Draft §9b: E123 craft mastery, E117 curiosity
  (practical), E119 legacy (multi-generational land)

**Research/documentation**:
- Helen & Scott Nearing (1954). "Living the Good Life" —
  foundational text, 60+ năm documentation
- Helen Nearing (1992). "Loving and Leaving the Good Life"
  — reflection at end of life
- Wendell Berry's extensive essay corpus (1970s-present),
  "The Unsettling of America" (1977) as key framework text
- Jenna Woginrich (2010). "Barnheart: The Incurable Longing
  for a Farm of One's Own"
- Brown (2011). "Back to the Land: The Enduring Dream of Self-
  Sufficiency in Modern America" — historical/sociological
- Academic: Kirschenmann et al. on sustainable agriculture
  communities; Brown & Schafft (2011) "Rural People and
  Communities in the 21st Century"
- YouTube documentation: contemporary homesteading channels
  (illustrative, not rigorous)

**Framework insights**:
1. **Multi-channel moderate dose beats single-channel extreme**:
   sustainability signature. Framework implication for optimal
   life design: distribute intake, don't maximize any one
   channel
2. **Embeddedness as channel amplifier**: feeds nature, living
   pattern, community, meaning simultaneously. Framework should
   consider embeddedness as structural variable, not individual
   channel
3. **Achievement channel is down-trainable**: homesteaders
   demonstrate that ambitious professionals CAN reduce
   conventional achievement demand if other channels compensate.
   Good news for framework "AI era life redesign" discussions
4. **Meaning channel + mastery channel + family = stable
   triad**: this combination appears robust across cultures
   (Berry Appalachian, Nearings New England, Japanese satoyama,
   Vietnamese rural tradition)
5. **Economic vs body-base distinction**: economic marginality
   does NOT translate to body-base marginality. Homesteaders
   often financially poor but body-base rich. Framework insight:
   modern economic metrics poorly track body-base health

**Notes**:
- Selection bias important: memoirs and documentation skew
  toward successful sustained cases. Drop-out cases less
  documented — framework should avoid romantic over-estimation
- Privilege distinction: many successful homesteaders have
  financial cushion, education, or second income enabling
  experiment. Pure subsistence homesteading (historically most
  farmers) often harder than memoirs suggest
- Children's experience variable: some report idyllic childhood,
  others report isolation or pressure. Parent-dependent
- 🟡 confidence: pattern well-documented but mix of memoir
  and academic; clean comparative data rare

---

### B9: Farmer / lifelong agricultural worker — Blue Zone adjacent 🟢

**Scenario**:
Individual born into agricultural family, works land 40-60+
năm — Vietnamese rice farmer, Italian vineyard farmer, Okinawan
garden keeper, Appalachian cattle rancher, etc. Daily routine
includes sunup-sundown outdoor labor, seasonal rhythm, community
embedded, multi-generational transmission. Distinguished from
B8 by origin (born into vs chose) and typical absence of
"back to land" ideology — this is just life, not project.

Particularly significant cases: **Blue Zone populations**
(Buettner 2008, 2012) — documented longevity hotspots correlate
strongly với lifelong agricultural community life. Sardinia
(Ogliastra shepherds), Okinawa (garden keepers), Ikaria (Greek
farmers), Nicoya (Costa Rica smallholders), Loma Linda
(Adventists including farmers) — all show centenarian rates
5-10x surrounding populations.

**Over-fed channel(s)**:
- **Movement** (§4.2.1): lifelong moderate physical work, never
  sedentary. Not exercise — functional movement embedded in
  life. Body-base channel fed as designed by evolution (varied,
  purposeful, daily)
- **Nature** (§4.2.2): daily outdoor across all seasons, weather
  immersion, deep knowledge of local ecology
- **Living pattern embedded** (§4.2.4): 40+ năm watching same
  land, same weather patterns, same animal cycles, same
  community people across lifespan — maximum embeddedness
- **Rhythmic structure**: circadian + seasonal + yearly cycles
  aligned với natural rhythms
- **Touch** (§4.2.5): soil, animals, tools, family, community
  — sustained rich tactile life
- **Meaning** (§4.3.3): feeding family, community, continuing
  tradition, often faith — meaning channel fed by rooted life
- **Social embedded**: same community across decades, deep
  recognition, "being missed when gone"
- **Mastery** (§4.3.4): tacit knowledge accumulation across
  decades — weather reading, soil, plants, animals

**Starved channel(s)**:
- **Economic stability**: agricultural economics often marginal,
  particularly smallholder
- **Formal education / intellectual breadth**: variable,
  sometimes limited
- **External novelty**: limited travel, limited new experiences
  — but compensated by seasonal variation within same place
- **Healthcare access**: rural populations sometimes underserved

**Consequences observed**:
- **Blue Zone longevity patterns**: centenarian rates 5-10x
  baseline documented across zones
- **Cognitive preservation**: Okinawa, Sardinia studies show
  lower dementia rates than urban controls
- **Cardiac health**: documented superior
- **Depression rates**: typically lower than urban comparison
  populations in same countries (though measurement caveats
  exist)
- **Physical toll**: joint wear, sun damage, specific
  occupational injuries — but distributed, chronic conditions
  emerge late
- **Subjective well-being**: generally reported high, though
  measurement methodology varies
- **Traditional cases dying out**: modernization displaces
  pattern; next generation often urbanizing, Blue Zones
  themselves shrinking

**Channel architecture revealed**:

Đây là case với strongest **empirical outcome data** cho
framework's silent channel hypothesis. Blue Zones provide
population-scale evidence that sustained multi-channel body-
base feeding correlates với longest documented healthy lifespans.
Không phải cherry-picked individuals — entire communities.

Critical insight: **the variables that correlate với Blue Zone
longevity are exactly the body-base channels framework predicts**:
- Daily natural movement (not exercise)
- Community embedded (not isolated)
- Meaningful work (not retirement ennui)
- Family integration (not age-segregated living)
- Natural food (channel §4.1.3)
- Low chronic stress
- Rhythmic structure (circadian + seasonal)
- Faith/meaning framework

**Hierarchy of evidence**: individual case studies (homesteader
memoirs) are suggestive; population-level data (Blue Zones)
is empirical confirmation. Framework should weight this as
highest-grade evidence for multi-channel body-base health
claim.

**Modernization displacement warning**: Blue Zones are shrinking
because economic integration changes lifestyle. Framework
implication: the body-base architecture that produces thriving
is actively being dismantled by modernization, not preserved.
This is a critical framework concern for AI era — if we don't
understand what we're losing, we can't preserve it consciously.

**Vietnamese relevance**: traditional Vietnamese rural life
(pre-industrial) shares channel structure với documented Blue
Zones — rice cultivation community embedded, daily physical
work, seasonal rhythm, family integration, Buddhist/ancestor
meaning. Pattern being dismantled currently as country
industrializes. Framework framework for preservation questions.

**Cross-reference**:
- Similar cases: B8 homesteader (chose version), B14 Vietnamese
  extended family (community channel emphasis), B27 craftsman
  (mastery compound), B46 Proenneke (solo version)
- Contrasting: B5 karoshi (opposite pattern, same culture
  different era), B1 workaholic (maximum industrial extraction),
  B6 nomad (movement without embeddedness)
- Body-Base.md: §4.2 silent channels full list, §4.3 higher-
  order channels, §10 cultural variation, §11 development
  trajectory (whole-life model)
- Feel-Example-Draft §9b: E123 (practical craft mastery), E119
  (generational legacy), E107 (meaning)

**Research/documentation**:
- Buettner, D. (2008). "The Blue Zones: Lessons for Living
  Longer From the People Who've Lived the Longest." National
  Geographic Books
- Buettner, D. (2012). "The Blue Zones: 9 Lessons for Living
  Longer." Expanded edition
- Poulain et al. (2004). "Identification of a geographic area
  characterized by extreme longevity in the Sardinia Island."
  Experimental Gerontology 39
- Willcox et al. (2007). Okinawa Centenarian Study. Journal of
  the American College of Nutrition 26
- Pes et al. (2013). "Male longevity in Sardinia: a review
  of historical sources." Journal of Biosocial Science 45
- Ngân 2013 và others on Vietnamese traditional rural
  psychosocial patterns (less available in English)
- Kaplan et al. (2017). "Coronary atherosclerosis in indigenous
  South American Tsimane: a cross-sectional cohort study."
  The Lancet 389 — related pattern, non-industrial population

**Framework insights**:
1. **Blue Zones = empirical validation**: population-level
   evidence that sustained multi-channel body-base feeding
   produces objectively better outcomes (longevity, cognition,
   mental health). Strongest framework support available
2. **Natural movement ≠ exercise**: functional movement
   embedded in daily life is architecturally different from
   gym exercise. Framework should distinguish these within
   §4.2.1 movement channel
3. **Embeddedness emerges as critical variable**: all Blue
   Zones share community embeddedness + land embeddedness.
   Framework should formalize embeddedness as channel quality
   modifier
4. **Modernization as silent deficit engine**: the processes
   that improve economic metrics often dismantle the body-
   base architecture Blue Zones demonstrate. Framework
   implication: economic development without body-base
   preservation is net loss
5. **Longevity as composite output**: framework predicts longevity
   should correlate với multi-channel feeding, not any single
   variable. Blue Zones confirm — no single magic variable,
   the pattern IS the finding

**Notes**:
- Measurement caveats: Blue Zone centenarian counts have been
  challenged (Newman 2024 preprint on pension fraud) — some
  claims may be overestimates. Framework should hold evidence
  provisionally but pattern still robust
- Selection biases: Blue Zone data self-selected by investigators
  looking for longevity, not randomized. Pattern robust but
  causal inference tentative
- Individual variation within Blue Zones: not everyone reaches
  100; pattern is population-level, not guarantee
- Cultural replication limits: cannot simply "install" Blue
  Zone pattern on unfamiliar population — pattern grew from
  local history. Framework emphasizes substrate principles,
  not cultural copy
- 🟢 confidence: extensive research, but evolving — hold
  specific claims loose, pattern claim robust

---

### B10: Ultra-marathon runner obsession — movement overfeed 🟡

**Scenario**:
Individual becomes deeply invested in extreme endurance running:
50-mile races, 100-mile races, multi-day ultras (Badwater,
UTMB, Barkley Marathons). Training 15-25+ miles/day, racing
monthly, entire life organized around training schedule. Pattern
typically emerges in 30s-40s, sometimes continuing into 60s+.
Documented extensively in books (Christopher McDougall "Born
to Run" 2009, Dean Karnazes "Ultramarathon Man" 2005, Scott
Jurek "Eat and Run" 2012, David Goggins "Can't Hurt Me" 2018).

Distinguished from B3 Olympic athlete by: amateur vs professional
(no Olympic endpoint, continuous engagement), from B7 extreme
sports by non-lethal (chronic damage not acute risk), from B9
farmer by voluntary vs embedded (chosen vs life context).

**Over-fed channel(s)**:
- **Movement** (§4.2.1): extreme dose — far exceeding evolved
  daily activity level. 2M năm evolved for 6-12 mile hunter-
  gatherer days; ultrarunner regularly 20-30+
- **Flow state** (§4.3.2): long-run flow sessions, hours of
  meditative movement
- **Endorphin loop**: well-documented "runner's high" — endogenous
  opioid + endocannabinoid system chronic activation
- **Mastery** (§4.3.4): specific skill development (pacing,
  nutrition, mental toughness, terrain reading)
- **Nature** (§4.2.2): trail running typically outdoor — partial
  nature channel compound
- **Identity**: self-concept fused với running identity
- **Community** (subtype): ultrarunning tribe provides agent
  channel specific compound

**Starved channel(s)**:
- **Deep rest** (§4.2.6): training volume precludes real rest
  — body always in recovery from last run
- **Body repair time**: joint cartilage, tendons, bones do
  not have time to fully repair between training loads
- **Relational time**: long training runs consume hours;
  social/family channel often squeezed
- **Caloric baseline** (§4.1.3): extreme training often
  incompatible với maintaining adequate caloric intake — REDs
  (Relative Energy Deficiency in Sport) documented
- **Female hormonal function** (gender-specific): female
  ultrarunners frequently develop amenorrhea từ training load

**Consequences observed**:
- **Chronic injuries**: stress fractures, tendonopathy, plantar
  fasciitis, hip/knee/back problems accumulating over decades
- **Cardiac remodeling**: endurance athlete heart changes —
  some protective, some potentially pathological (atrial
  fibrillation risk elevated in lifetime endurance athletes,
  per Andersen et al. 2013)
- **Overtraining syndrome**: chronic fatigue, depression,
  performance decline, hormonal dysregulation — can take
  months to years to recover
- **REDs consequences**: bone loss, hormonal dysfunction,
  immunosuppression
- **When forced to stop (injury)**: many report depression,
  withdrawal-like state — "can't run" = identity crisis +
  endorphin withdrawal
- **Mental health**: mixed data — running benefits general
  population well-established; extreme dose shows different
  pattern với overtraining-related depression

**Channel architecture revealed**:

Đây là case critical cho framework claim rằng **any channel can
be over-fed, including "beneficial" ones**. Movement channel
is essential body-base need — but extreme dose produces
damage like any over-feeding. Framework correction to naive
"movement good = more movement better" logic.

**Evolutionary mismatch mechanism**: human body evolved for
6-12 mile daily hunter-gatherer activity. Ultrarunner dose
exceeds evolved calibration by 2-5x sustained. Framework
implication: evolved calibration has both floor AND ceiling.
Deficit and excess both produce body-base dysfunction.

**Flow channel as addictive pathway**: runner's high and flow
state access through running can produce addiction-like pattern
— withdrawal symptoms when forced to stop validate endorphin
system dependency. Framework insight: flow access pathways
vary in addictivity; endurance running appears high.

**Movement ≠ farmer's movement**: B9 farmer and B10 ultramarathoner
both have high movement channel dose, but different structures
— farmer's movement is varied, functional, sustained lifelong,
moderate intensity; ultramarathoner's is repetitive, extreme,
peak-intensity. Same channel, different sub-feeding patterns.
Outcomes differ dramatically. Framework should distinguish
**dose pattern** within movement channel, not just volume.

**"Identity fusion" pattern present**: like B3 Olympic, many
ultrarunners report identity fusion với sport. When injury
forces cessation, identity crisis parallels post-Olympic pattern.
Single-channel identity fusion is architecturally risky
regardless of which channel.

**Cross-reference**:
- Similar cases: B3 Olympic (elite version), B7 extreme sports
  (lethal variant), B1 workaholic (similar over-feed structure,
  different channel)
- Contrasting: B9 farmer (sustainable movement dose), B4
  balanced founder (moderate movement within multi-channel)
- Body-Base.md: §4.2.1 movement (dose pattern refinement),
  §4.3.2 flow, §5 signal timeline (over-feeding not just
  under-feeding)
- Feel-Example-Draft §9b: E122 flow, E118 obsessive inquiry
  (applied to training)

**Research/documentation**:
- McDougall, C. (2009). "Born to Run: A Hidden Tribe,
  Superathletes, and the Greatest Race the World Has Never
  Seen"
- Karnazes, D. (2005). "Ultramarathon Man"
- Jurek, S. (2012). "Eat and Run"
